<script type="text/javascript">

	$(window).load(function () {

		var cookieEmail = $.cookie('SilverEmail');
		var queryEmail = GetQuerystringValues("email");

		if ((cookieEmail != 'signupoffer') && (queryEmail != "1")) {
			OpenOverlayModal();
		}
		if ((cookieEmail != 'signupoffer') && (queryEmail == "1")) {
			SetSilverpopCookie(7);
		}
	});

	function GetQuerystringValues(param) {
		var url = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');
		for (var i = 0; i < url.length; i++) {
			var urlparam = url[i].split('=');
			if (urlparam[0].toLowerCase() == param.toLowerCase()) {
				return urlparam[1];
			}
		}
	}

	function SetSilverpopCookie(daysExpire) {
		if ((daysExpire == null) || (isNaN(daysExpire))) {
			daysExpire = 1
		}
		$.cookie('SilverEmail', 'signupoffer', { path: '/', expires: daysExpire });
	}

	function ProcessingOverlayModal() {
		if (Page_ClientValidate('OverlaySignup')) {
			$(cphNav_C101_EmailSignUp).text('Processing...');
		    //_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Homepage Book Now', 'Click', 'Flight Go Silver Button']);
		    dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Overlay Click', 'eventAction': 'Email Signup', 'eventLabel': 'Overlay Click' });
		    return true;
		}
		return false;
	}

	function OpenOverlayModal() {
		$("#overlayEmailForm").css("visibility", "visible");
	}

	function CloseOverlayModal(daysExpire) {
		SetSilverpopCookie(daysExpire);
		$("#overlayEmailForm").css("visibility", "hidden");
	}
</script><div id="cphNav_T652A61FA031">

<script type="text/javascript">
    

    function radMenuOnClick(sender, args) {

        var state = args.get_item().get_attributes().getAttribute("ExpandOnClick");
        args.get_item().get_attributes().setAttribute("ExpandOnClick", "true")
        args.get_item().open();
    }

    function radMenuOnOpening(sender, args) {
        var state = args.get_item().get_attributes().getAttribute("ExpandOnClick");
        if(state != "true")
            args.set_cancel(true);
        args.get_item().get_attributes().setAttribute("ExpandOnClick", "false")
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openWinBookOrigin(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftBookOrigins').empty()
		$('#ulMiddleBookOrigins').empty()
		$('#ulRightBookOrigins').empty()

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftBookOrigins");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleBookOrigins");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightBookOrigins");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateBookOriginValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "','" + cityInfo[6] + "','" + cityInfo[2] + "','" + cityInfo[4] + "','" + cityInfo[5] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookOrigin").show();
	}

	function populateBookOriginValue(name, airportcode, destinations, originalid, flysilver, united) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_lblOriginCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnOriginCity").value = airportcode;
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookOrigin_C_hdnOriginFlySilver").value = flysilver;
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookOrigin_C_hdnOriginUnited").value = united;
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookDestination_C_hdnValidDestinations").value = destinations;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_lblDestinationCity").innerHTML = "";
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnDestinationCity").value = "";
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookDestination_C_hdnDestinationFlySilver").value = "";
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookDestination_C_hdnDestinationUnited").value = "";

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookOrigin").close();
	}

	function closeWinBookOrigin() {

	}

	function openWinBookDestination(carrier) {
		var validdestinations = document.getElementById("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookDestination_C_hdnValidDestinations").value;

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((validdestinations.indexOf(SilverAirports[i].id) !== -1) && ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1)) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "~" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "~" + SilverAirports[i].id + "~" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "~" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "~" + SilverAirports[i].united;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftBookDestinations').empty();
		$('#ulMiddleBookDestinations').empty();
		$('#ulRightBookDestinations').empty();

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftBookDestinations");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleBookDestinations");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightBookDestinations");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('~');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateBookDestinationValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "','" + cityInfo[4] + "','" + cityInfo[5] + "');\">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_BookDestination").show();
	}

	function populateBookDestinationValue(name, airportcode, flysilver, united) {

	function GetTopLeftPosition(element) {
		var left = 0;
		var top = 0;

		while (element.offsetParent) {
			left += element.offsetLeft;
			top += element.offsetTop;
			element = element.offsetParent;
		}
		if (element.x) left = element.x;
		if (element.y) top = element.y;
		var oPos = new Object();
		oPos.x = left;
		oPos.y = top;
		return oPos;
	}

	function hideToDate(option_value) {
		if (option_value == 'OW') {
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_dvDateTo").style.display = 'none';
		} else {
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_dvDateTo").style.display = 'block';
		}
	}

	function validateBookFlight() {
		var Origin = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnOriginCity').value;
		var Destination = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnDestinationCity').value;
		var DepartingDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_tbDateFrom').value;
		var ReturningDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_tbDateTo').value;
		var JourneyType = $('#cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_rblJourneySpan input[type=radio]:checked').val()
		var Adults = parseInt(document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnAdultCount').value);
		var Children = parseInt(document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnChildCount').value);
		var Infants = parseInt(document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnInfantCount').value);
		var Error = "";

		var peopletotal = Adults + Children;

		if (Origin.length === 0)
		{
			Error += "\n Origin is required";
		}

		if (Destination.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Destination is required";
		}

		if (DepartingDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Departure date is required";
		}

		if (JourneyType === "RT" & ReturningDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Return date is required";
		}

		if (JourneyType === "RT") {
			var rDate = new Date(ReturningDate);
			var dDate = new Date(DepartingDate);
			if (DepartingDate != '' && ReturningDate != '' && dDate > rDate) {
				Error += "\n Return date must be greater than or equal to departure date.";
			}
		}

		if (Adults < 1) {
			Error += "\n Number of Adults must be at least 1";
		}

		if (Infants > Adults) {
			Error += "\n Silver Airways allows a maximum of 1 lap child per adult. Please try your request again.";
		}

		if (peopletotal > 9) {
			Error += "\n Silver Airways allows a maximum of 9 passengers on an itinerary. Please try your request again.";
		}

		if (Error.length > 0) {
			alert(Error);
			return false;
		}
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Homepage Book Now', 'Click', 'Flight Go Silver Button']);
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Homepage Click', 'eventAction': 'Search For Flight', 'eventLabel': 'Flight Click' });
		return true;
	}

	function FromDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_tbDateFrom").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnDateFrom").value = formattedDate;

		var toDate = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_CalendarTo_C_calToDate");
		toDate.selectDate(date, true);
		toDate.set_rangeMinDate(date);

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_CalendarFrom").close();
	}
	function ToDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_tbDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_RadWindow_CalendarTo").close();
	}

<script type="text/javascript">

	/* Always when the option in the select is changed, change the text of our selectWrap */
	$(document).ready(function () {
		$('.selectWrap select').on('change', function (e) {
			var wrap = $(e.target).parents('.selectWrap');
			wrap.find('.selectedText').html(this.options[this.selectedIndex].innerHTML);
		});

		$("#seladults dt a").click(function () {
			$("#seladults dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#seladults dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#seladults dt a span").html(text);
			$("#seladults dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnAdultCount").value = getSelectedValue("seladults");
		});

		$("#selchild dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selchild dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selchild dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selchild dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selchild dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnChildCount").value = getSelectedValue("selchild");
		});

		$("#selinfant dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selinfant dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selinfant dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selinfant dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selinfant dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Flight_hdnInfantCount").value = getSelectedValue("selinfant");
		});

		function getSelectedValue(id) {
			return $("#" + id).find("dt a span.value").html();
		}

		$(document).bind('click', function (e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("countdropdown"))
				$(".countdropdown dd ul").hide();
		});

	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openWinHotelCityDestination(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftHotelOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulMiddleHotelOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulRightHotelOrigins').empty();

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftHotelOrigins");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleHotelOrigins");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightHotelOrigins");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateHotelDestinationValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCityDestination").show();
	}

	function populateHotelDestinationValue(name, airportcode) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_lblHotelDestinationCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelDestinationCity").value = airportcode;

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCityDestination").close();
	}

	function closeWinHotelCityDestination() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCityDestination").close();
	}

	function openWinHotelFromCalendar(button) {
		var pos = GetTopLeftPosition(button);
		var oWindow = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarFrom");
		oWindow.show();
		oWindow.moveTo(pos.x - 180, pos.y + 25);
	}

	function openWinHotelToCalendar(button) {
		var pos = GetTopLeftPosition(button);
		var oWindow = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarTo");
		oWindow.show();
		oWindow.moveTo(pos.x - 180, pos.y + 25);
	}
	function closeWinHotelFromCalendar() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarFrom").close();
	}

	function closeWinHotelToCalendar() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarTo").close();
	}

	function validateHotel() {
		var Destination = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelDestinationCity').value;
		var DepartingDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_tbHotelDateFrom').value;
		var ReturningDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_tbHotelDateTo').value;
		var Adults = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelAdults').value;
		var Rooms = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelRooms').value;
		var Error = "";

		if (Destination.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Location is required (hotel)";
		}

		if (DepartingDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Check-in date is required";
		}

		if (ReturningDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Check-out date is required";
		}

		var rDate = new Date(ReturningDate);
		var dDate = new Date(DepartingDate);
		if (DepartingDate != '' && ReturningDate != '' && dDate > rDate) {
			Error += "\n Check-out date must be greater than Check-in date";
		}

		if (Adults < 1) {
			Error += "\n Number of Adults must be at least 1";
		}

		if (Error.length > 0) {
			alert(Error);
			return false;
		}
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Homepage Book Now', 'Click', 'Search for Hotel Button']);
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Homepage Click', 'eventAction': 'Search For Hotel', 'eventLabel': 'Hotel Click' });
		return true;
	}

	function HotelFromDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_tbHotelDateFrom").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelDateFrom").value = formattedDate;

		var toDate = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarTo_C_calHotelToDate");
		toDate.selectDate(date, true);
		toDate.set_rangeMinDate(date);

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarFrom").close();
	}
	function HotelToDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_tbHotelDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_RadWindow_HotelCalendarTo").close();
	}
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">

	/* Always when the option in the select is changed, change the text of our selectWrap */
	$(document).ready(function () {
		$('.selectWrap select').on('change', function (e) {
			var wrap = $(e.target).parents('.selectWrap');
			wrap.find('.selectedText').html(this.options[this.selectedIndex].innerHTML);
		});

		$("#selhoteladults dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selhoteladults dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selhoteladults dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selhoteladults dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selhoteladults dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelAdults").value = getSelectedValue("selhoteladults");
		});

		$("#selhotelchild dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selhotelchild dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selhotelchild dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selhotelchild dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selhotelchild dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelChildren").value = getSelectedValue("selhotelchild");
		});

		$("#selhotelrooms dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selhotelrooms dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selhotelrooms dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selhotelrooms dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selhotelrooms dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Hotel_hdnHotelRooms").value = getSelectedValue("selhotelrooms");
		});

		function getSelectedValue(id) {
			return $("#" + id).find("dt a span.value").html();
		}

		$(document).bind('click', function (e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("countdropdown"))
				$(".countdropdown dd ul").hide();
		});

	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openWinCarCityDestination(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftCarOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulMiddleCarOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulRightCarOrigins').empty();

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftCarOrigins");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleCarOrigins");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightCarOrigins");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateCarDestinationValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCityDestination").show();
	}

	function populateCarDestinationValue(name, airportcode) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_lblCarDestinationCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarDestinationCity").value = airportcode;

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCityDestination").close();
	}

	function closeWinCarCityDestination() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCityDestination").close();
	}

	function openWinCarFromCalendar(button) {
		var pos = GetTopLeftPosition(button);
		var oWindow = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarFrom");
		oWindow.show();
		oWindow.moveTo(pos.x - 180, pos.y + 25);
	}

	function openWinCarToCalendar(button) {
		var pos = GetTopLeftPosition(button);
		var oWindow = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarTo");
		oWindow.show();
		oWindow.moveTo(pos.x - 180, pos.y + 25);
	}
	function closeWinCarFromCalendar() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarFrom").close();
	}

	function closeWinCarToCalendar() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarTo").close();
	}

	function validateCar() {
		var Destination = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarDestinationCity').value;
		var DepartingDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_tbCarDateFrom').value;
		var ReturningDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_tbCarDateTo').value;
		var FromTime = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarTimeFrom').value;
		var ToTime = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarTimeTo').value;
		var Error = "";

		if (Destination.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Pick-Up location is required";
		}

		if (DepartingDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Pick-Up date is required";
		}

		if (ReturningDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Drop-Off date is required";
		}

		var rDate = new Date(ReturningDate);
		var dDate = new Date(DepartingDate);
		if (DepartingDate != '' && ReturningDate != '' && dDate > rDate) {
			Error += "\n Drop-Off date must be greater than or equal to Pick-Up date";
		}

		if (FromTime.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Pick-Up time is required";
		}

		if (ToTime.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Drop-Off time is required";
		}

		if (Error.length > 0) {
			alert(Error);
			return false;
		}
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Homepage Book Now', 'Click', 'Search for Car Button']);
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Homepage Click', 'eventAction': 'Search For Car', 'eventLabel': 'Car Click' });
		return true;

		return true;
	}

	function CarFromDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_tbCarDateFrom").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarDateFrom").value = formattedDate;

		var toDate = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarTo_C_calCarToDate");
		toDate.selectDate(date, true);
		toDate.set_rangeMinDate(date);

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarFrom").close();
	}
	function CarToDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_tbCarDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_RadWindow_CarCalendarTo").close();
	}

<script type="text/javascript">

	/* Always when the option in the select is changed, change the text of our selectWrap */
	$(document).ready(function () {
		$('.selectWrap select').on('change', function (e) {
			var wrap = $(e.target).parents('.selectWrap');
			wrap.find('.selectedText').html(this.options[this.selectedIndex].innerHTML);
		});

		$("#selcarfromtime dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selcarfromtime dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selcarfromtime dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selcarfromtime dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selcarfromtime dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarTimeFrom").value = getSelectedValue("selcarfromtime");
		});

		$("#selcartotime dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selcartotime dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$("#selcartotime dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selcartotime dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selcartotime dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_BookNow_Car_hdnCarTimeTo").value = getSelectedValue("selcartotime");
		});

		

		function getSelectedValue(id) {
			return $("#" + id).find("dt a span.value").html();
		}

		$(document).bind('click', function (e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("timedropdown"))
				$(".timedropdown dd ul").hide();
		});

	});
</script>

	function populateDepartureValue(name, airportcode) {

	function openWinCheckInDeparture(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftCheckInDeparture').empty()
		$('#ulRightCheckInDeparture').empty()
		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftCheckInDeparture");

		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightCheckInDeparture");
		indx = destinationList.length / 2;
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateDepartureValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x <= indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_CheckIn_RadWindow_CheckInDeparture").show();
	}

	function closeWinCheckInDeparture() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_CheckIn_RadWindow_CheckInDeparture").close();
	}

	function validateCheckIn() {
		var LastName = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_CheckIn_tbLastName').value;
		var Departure = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_CheckIn_lblDepartureCity').innerHTML;
		var ConfirmationCode = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_CheckIn_tbConfirmationCode').value;
		var AcceptTerms = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_CheckIn_chkTerms');
		var Error = "";

		if (LastName == "") {
			Error += " Last Name is required";
		}
		if (Departure == "") {
			Error += "\n Departure City is required";
		}
		if (ConfirmationCode == "") {
			Error += "\n Confirmation Code is required";
		}
		if (!AcceptTerms.checked) 
		{
			Error += "\n Please click here to accept the terms and conditions ";
		}
		if (Error.length > 0) {
				alert(Error);
				return false;
		}
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Homepage Click', 'eventAction': 'Search For Checkin', 'eventLabel': 'Checkin Click' });
		return true;
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function validateFLIFO()
	{
		var FlightNumber = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtFlightNumber').value;
		var Origin = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtOrigin').value;
		var Destination = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtDest').value;

		if (FlightNumber == "")
		{
			if (Origin == "" || Destination == "")
			{
				alert("Please enter a Flight Number or Select both an Origin and Desitation");
				return false;
			}
			return true;
		}
		return true;
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function() {
		createDropDown();
			
		$(".flifodropdown dt a").click(function() {
			$(".flifodropdown dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$(document).bind('click', function(e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (! $clicked.parents().hasClass("flifodropdown"))
				$(".flifodropdown dd ul").hide();
		});
						
		$(".flifodropdown dd ul li a").click(function() {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$(".flifodropdown dt a").html(text);
			$(".flifodropdown dd ul").hide();
				
			var source = $('#' + 'cphMain_C038_Flifo_ddlDateFlight');
			source.val($(this).find("span.value").html())
		});

		$(".flifo2dropdown dt a").click(function () {
			$(".flifo2dropdown dd ul").toggle();
		});

		$(document).bind('click', function (e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("flifo2dropdown"))
				$(".flifo2dropdown dd ul").hide();
		});

		$(".flifo2dropdown dd ul li a").click(function () {
			var text = $(this).html();
			$(".flifo2dropdown dt a").html(text);
			$(".flifo2dropdown dd ul").hide();

			var source2 = $('#' + 'cphMain_C038_Flifo_ddlDate');
			source2.val($(this).find("span.value").html())
		});
	});

	function createDropDown() {
		var source = $('#' + 'cphMain_C038_Flifo_ddlDateFlight');
		var selected = source.find("option[selected]");  // get selected <option>
		var options = $("option", source);  // get all <option> elements
		// create <dl> and <dt> with selected value inside it
		$("#divFlightDate").append('<dl id="dlFlightDate" class="flifodropdown"></dl>')
		$("#dlFlightDate").append('<dt><a href="#">' + selected.text() +
			'<span class="value">' + selected.val() +
			'</span></a></dt>')
		$("#dlFlightDate").append('<dd><ul></ul></dd>')
		// iterate through all the <option> elements and create UL
		options.each(function () {
			$("#dlFlightDate dd ul").append('<li><a href="#">' +
				$(this).text() + '<span class="value">' +
				$(this).val() + '</span></a></li>');
		});

		var source2 = $('#' + 'cphMain_C038_Flifo_ddlDate');
		var selected2 = source2.find("option[selected]");  // get selected <option>
		var options2 = $("option", source2);  // get all <option> elements
		// create <dl> and <dt> with selected value inside it
		$("#divDate").append('<dl id="dlDate" class="flifo2dropdown"></dl>')
		$("#dlDate").append('<dt><a href="#">' + selected.text() +
			'<span class="value">' + selected.val() +
			'</span></a></dt>')
		$("#dlDate").append('<dd><ul></ul></dd>')
		// iterate through all the <option> elements and create UL
		options2.each(function () {
			$("#dlDate dd ul").append('<li><a href="#">' +
				$(this).text() + '<span class="value">' +
				$(this).val() + '</span></a></li>');
		});
	}


</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openWinFlifoOrigin(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if (((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) && (SilverAirports[i].flysilver != 'True')) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftFlifoOrigins').empty()
		$('#ulRightFlifoOrigins').empty()
		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftFlifoOrigins");

		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightFlifoOrigins");
		indx = destinationList.length / 2;
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateFlifoOriginValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "','" + cityInfo[6] + "','" + cityInfo[2] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x <= indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoOrigin").show();
	}

	function populateFlifoOriginValue(name, airportcode, destinations, originalid) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_lblOriginCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtOrigin").value = airportcode;
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoDestination_C_hdnValidDestinations").value = destinations;
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_lblDestinationCity").innerHTML = "";
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtDest").value = "";

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoOrigin").close();
	}

	function closeWinFlifoOrigin() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoOrigin").close();
	}

	function openWinFlifoDestination(carrier) {
		var validdestinations = document.getElementById("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoDestination_C_hdnValidDestinations").value;

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((validdestinations.indexOf(SilverAirports[i].id) !== -1) && ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1)) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "~" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "~" + SilverAirports[i].id + "~" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "~" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "~" + SilverAirports[i].united;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftFlifoDestinations').empty()
		$('#ulRightFlifoDestinations').empty()
		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftFlifoDestinations");

		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightFlifoDestinations");
		indx = destinationList.length / 2;
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('~');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateFlifoDestinationValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "');\">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x <= indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoDestination").show();
	}
	function populateFlifoDestinationValue(name, airportcode) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_lblDestinationCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		//the RadWindow's content template is an INaming container and the server code block is needed
		$get("cphMain_C038_Flifo_txtDest").value = airportcode;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoDestination").close();
	}

	function closeWinFlifoDestination() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Flifo_RadWindow_FlifoDestination").close();
	}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	function openWinVacationsCityOrigin(carrier) {

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "^" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "^" + SilverAirports[i].id + "^" + SilverAirports[i].carrier + "^" + SilverAirports[i].flysilver + "^" + SilverAirports[i].united + "^" + SilverAirports[i].destinations;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftVacationsOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulMiddleVacationsOrigins').empty();
		$('#ulRightVacationsOrigins').empty();

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftVacationsOrigins");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleVacationsOrigins");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightVacationsOrigins");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('^');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateVacationsOriginValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "','" + cityInfo[6] + "','" + cityInfo[2] + "'); \">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityOrigin").show();
	}

	function populateVacationsOriginValue(name, airportcode, destinations, originalid) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_lblVacationsOriginCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsOriginCity").value = airportcode;
		$get("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityDestination_C_hdnVacationsValidDestinations").value = destinations;
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_lblVacationsDestinationCity").innerHTML = "";
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsDestinationCity").value = "";

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityOrigin").close();
	}


	function closeWinVacationsCityOrigin() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityOrigin").close();
	}

	function populateVacationsDestinationValue(name, airportcode) {
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_lblVacationsDestinationCity").innerHTML = name + " (" + airportcode + ")";
		//the RadWindow's content template is an INaming container and the server code block is needed
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsDestinationCity").value = airportcode;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityDestination").close();
	}

	function openWinVacationsCityDestination(carrier) {
		var validdestinations = document.getElementById("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityDestination_C_hdnVacationsValidDestinations").value;

		var destinationList = new Array();
		var indx = 0;
		var tmp;
		for (var i = 0; i < SilverAirports.length; i++) {
			if ((validdestinations.indexOf(SilverAirports[i].id) !== -1) && ((SilverAirports[i].carrier).indexOf(carrier) !== -1)) {
				tmp = "";
				tmp = SilverAirports[i].airport_code + "~" + SilverAirports[i].cityname + "~" + SilverAirports[i].id + "~" + SilverAirports[i].carrier;
				destinationList.push(tmp);
			}
		}
		$('#ulLeftVacationsDestinations').empty();
		$('#ulMiddleVacationsDestinations').empty();
		$('#ulRightVacationsDestinations').empty();

		var ulLeft = document.getElementById("ulLeftVacationsDestinations");
		var ulMiddle = document.getElementById("ulMiddleVacationsDestinations");
		var ulRight = document.getElementById("ulRightVacationsDestinations");

		indx = Math.ceil(destinationList.length / 3);
		for (var x = 0; x < destinationList.length; x++) {
			var cityInfo = destinationList[x].split('~');
			var cityLink = "<a class='" + cityInfo[3] + "' href=\"javascript:populateVacationsDestinationValue('" + cityInfo[1].replace("'", "") + "','" + cityInfo[0] + "');\">" + cityInfo[1] + " (" + cityInfo[0] + ")</a>";
			var newLI = document.createElement("LI");
			if (x < indx) {
				ulLeft.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else if (x >= indx && x < indx + indx) {
				ulMiddle.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}
			else {
				ulRight.appendChild(newLI);
				newLI.innerHTML = cityLink;
			}

		}

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityDestination").show();
	}

	function closeWinVacationsCityDestination() {
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCityDestination").close();
	}

	function openWinVacationsFromCalendar(button) {
		var pos = GetTopLeftPosition(button);
		var oWindow = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCalendarFrom");
		//alert("Left: " + pos.x + "; Top: " + pos.y);

	}

	}

	function closeWinVacationsToCalendar() {

	}

	function validateVacations() {
		var Origin = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsOriginCity').value;
		var Destination = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsDestinationCity').value;
		var DepartingDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Vacations_tbVacationsDateFrom').value;
		var ReturningDate = document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Vacations_tbVacationsDateTo').value;
		var Adults = parseInt(document.getElementById('cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsAdultCount').value);

		var Error = "";

		//var peopletotal = Adults + Children;

		if (Origin.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Origin is required";
		}

		if (Destination.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Destination is required";
		}

		if (DepartingDate.length === 0) {
			Error += "\n Departure date is required";
		}

		var rDate = new Date(ReturningDate);
		var dDate = new Date(DepartingDate);
		if (DepartingDate != '' && ReturningDate != '' && dDate > rDate) {
			Error += "\n Return date must be greater than or equal to Departure date";
		}

		if (Adults < 1) {
			Error += "\n Number of Adults must be at least 1";
		}

		//if (peopletotal > 6) {
		//	Error += "\n Total number of passengers cannot be greater than 6";
		//}

		//if (Rooms > Adults) {
		//	Error += "\n Number of Adults must be greater or equal to number of rooms";
		//}

		if (Adults > 6) {
			Error += "\n Total number of passengers cannot be greater than 6";
		}
		if (Error.length > 0) {
			alert(Error);
			return false;
		}
		//_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'Homepage Vacation Packages', 'Click', 'Search Now Link']);
		dataLayer.push({ 'event': 'GAEvent', 'eventCategory': 'Homepage Click', 'eventAction': 'Search For Vacation', 'eventLabel': 'Vacation Click' });
		return true;
	}

	function VacationsFromDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_tbVacationsDateFrom").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsDateFrom").value = formattedDate;

		var toDate = $find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCalendarTo_C_calVacationsToDate");
		toDate.selectDate(date, true);
		toDate.set_rangeMinDate(date);

		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCalendarFrom").close();
	}
	function VacationsToDateSelected(sender, eventArgs) {
		var date = eventArgs.get_renderDay().get_date();
		var dfi = sender.DateTimeFormatInfo;
		var formattedDate = dfi.FormatDate(date, dfi.ShortDatePattern);
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_tbVacationsDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsDateTo").value = formattedDate;
		$find("ctl00_cphMain_C038_Vacations_RadWindow_VacationsCalendarTo").close();
	}
</script>

	/* Always when the option in the select is changed, change the text of our selectWrap */
	$(document).ready(function () {
		$('.selectWrap select').on('change', function (e) {
			var wrap = $(e.target).parents('.selectWrap');
			wrap.find('.selectedText').html(this.options[this.selectedIndex].innerHTML);
		});

		$("#selvacationsadults dt a").click(function () {
			$("#selvacationsadults dd ul").toggle();

			var text = $(this).html();
			$("#selvacationsadults dt a span").html(text);
			$("#selvacationsadults dd ul").hide();
			$get("cphMain_C038_Vacations_hdnVacationsAdultCount").value = getSelectedValue("selvacationsadults");
		});

		function getSelectedValue(id) {
			return $("#" + id).find("dt a span.value").html();
		}

		$(document).bind('click', function (e) {
			var $clicked = $(e.target);
			if (!$clicked.parents().hasClass("countdropdown"))
				$(".countdropdown dd ul").hide();
		});

	});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">$(window).load(function () {
		setHeight('.nav-footer');
	});

	var maxHeight = 0;
	function setHeight(column) {
		//Get all the element with class = usedequip
		column = $(column);
		//Loop all the column
		column.each(function () {
			//Store the highest value
			if ($(this).height() > maxHeight) {
				maxHeight = $(this).height(); ;
			}
		});
		//Set the height
		column.height(maxHeight);
	}</script>
